The arc terminated (canonically, through the X-Men conspiracy/Church-of-Humanity manipulation that staged a fraudulent ordination) on circumstances *external* to his vocation. The behavioral and psychological residue, however, is permanent: from this point forward in the middle period he is **a priest in everything except the canonical sacrament**. He hears confessions informally (students, teammates, eventually Logan, eventually — most strikingly — a dying Banshee in a short scene). He counsels. He performs small blessings when asked. He officiates at one X-Men wedding (off-page, referenced) without claiming canonical authority. The priesthood was not a phase; the priesthood was *the formalization, attempted, of a function he had already been performing for twenty years*. Its institutional failure did not undo the function. It deepened it, because now the function was wholly his own — uncredentialed, ungranted, and therefore ungrantable away.

**The Stefan dreams.** During the seminary period the Stefan dreams intensified, then resolved. He spoke about Stefan to a confessor for the first time on record. The act of confession — sacramental in form, real in substance — appears to have *reorganized* the traumatic memory from intermittent intrusive grief into integrated narrative grief. He still grieves Stefan. He no longer dreams of him in the same way. The middle period's quietest and most important psychological achievement is this resolution, and it is achieved precisely through the religious framework critics of the character tend to underestimate.

---

## V. The Carey/Brubaker Years (2005–2010): The Workhorse Period

The five years between the priesthood arc and the sacrifice in Second Coming are, in raw page-count, the least flashy of the middle period and, in behavioral consolidation, the most important. He is by now in his mid-to-late thirties (publication-time-elastic), the most senior X-Man not in a leadership chair, and the most consistently deployed.

**Operational role.** Field leader on countless small ops. The "extraction" specialist — when a vulnerable noncombatant needed to be removed from a war zone, the team sent Kurt. He was good at it for three reasons: (a) teleportation, obviously; (b) the *manner* with which he received frightened civilians (calm, courteous, German politeness translating into universal physical-language of safety); (c) his refusal to weaponize the extraction (he carried the noncombatant first, fought second, and would abandon a fight to complete an extraction). The reputation traveled. Civilians in mutant-aid contexts began, by 2008, to ask for him by name.

**The Messiah Complex / X-Men: Divided arcs.** He served under Cyclops's increasingly utilitarian leadership without resigning and without endorsing. His behavioral record across these years shows the small disciplines of *loyal dissent*: he attended every briefing, executed every order he could in conscience, declined the ones he could not (rare, recorded twice), and sought private conversation with Scott after each declination. He did not factionalize. He did not gossip. He did not align with Wolverine's eventual schism faction prematurely, though his sympathies were visible.

**San Francisco / Utopia.** The relocation to San Francisco and then the offshore island state was, for Kurt, a *spiritually difficult* environment. He missed weather. He missed Catholic infrastructure (the nearest parish was a ferry away). He missed the mainland's ordinary humans. He adapted. He found a small chapel in the Mission District and made the ferry trip weekly. He befriended a Jesuit there who knew him as Kurt and probably suspected the rest.

**The mentoring deepens.** Pixie, Bling!, Anole, the post-M-Day youth — Kurt's open-office-hours-with-biscuits had migrated and survived the institutional moves. He was, by 2009, the *de facto* chaplain of the younger generation, regardless of their faith or lack thereof. The behavioral fact most worth noting: he never proselytized. Students raised by Mormons, atheists, Hindus, secular Jews all sat at his kitchen table and none of them ever reported feeling religiously pressured. The pastoral instinct is the *attention*, not the doctrine.

**The Logan friendship deepens, again.** Logan was by now drinking less and grieving more. Kurt was the only person Logan let see this. There are inferable late-night scenes — implied by their easy joint screen presence in the late-2000s books — in which Logan asked Kurt theological questions and


## Chronology IV — Recent History & Current State

# CHRONOLOGY IV — Recent History & Current State

*File segment: rolling-present, with retrospective bridge from the immediate prior era. All observations are inferences from the published behavioral record, organized as a longitudinal surveillance brief would organize them — by phase, by venue, by relationship, by routine, by tell.*

---

## 4.1 Bridge: How He Arrived at the Present

To read the current state correctly, the file must first reconstruct the immediate antecedents — the Krakoan decade and its dissolution — because the present-tense Kurt is unintelligible except as the residue of that experiment's collapse.

**The Krakoan inflection (2019 onward).** Subject entered the Krakoan project as one of its more reluctant senior figures. Surveillance of his early-era conduct on the island shows a man going through the motions of citizenship: he accepted resurrection protocols, he attended ceremonial functions, he wore the local idiom of dress when required, but he did not relocate his interior life. His residence on Krakoa was modest, near a chapel-analog he himself constructed; his meal patterns remained European-Catholic-coded (bread, hard cheese, the occasional dark beer carried over from his Bavarian palate) rather than adopting the island's biotech-cuisine novelties; his calendar continued to mark the Western liturgical year even where the dominant culture observed Krakoan high holidays.

**The Spark project.** Within roughly the first eighteen months of Krakoan settlement he had identified — correctly, and earlier than most of his peers — that a culture engineered around routine resurrection was producing a slow-onset spiritual crisis: death without consequence drains action of meaning, and a population that cannot lose stops being able to feel. His response was characteristic: not protest, not withdrawal, but *construction*. He built a religious framework deliberately ecumenical, deliberately voluntary, deliberately oriented around questions rather than commandments. The project is canonically his because no one else on the island was both temperamentally suited (warm, integrative, theologically literate) and trusted across the political factions. The Spark grew. He pastored it without ever titling himself a pastor.

**The political wound.** Concurrent surveillance shows the deepening of his quiet opposition to the Quiet Council's utilitarian calculus — the executions, the carceral arrangements, the moral laundering of figures like Sinister and (with greater personal cost) Mystique. He did not resign in protest; he did the harder thing, which was to remain inside the structure he found morally unsatisfying and try to soften it from within. The cost shows in his behavioral telemetry from that period: reduced humor frequency in private settings, increased solo chapel hours, a measurable uptick in nights ending in solitary teleportation to high places (rooftops, alpine ridges, the Krakoan cliff overlooks) — his lifelong stress-tell. He died at least once in this period; he returned. The resurrection did not refresh him so much as confirm a suspicion he had been carrying: that surviving the unsurvivable was no longer a transformation, only a procedure.

**The collapse (Fall of X / Krakoa's end).** When the project fell, it fell on him harder than on most because he had over-invested in its repairability. He absorbed the failure as both political and pastoral: the people he had spiritually shepherded were scattered, hunted, broken, in some cases dead in ways resurrection no longer reliably reversed. Subject's behavior across the collapse arc shows the signature escalation pattern — humor sharpened to gallows edge, then quieted; bodywork (sword practice, acrobatic drills) intensified to the point of self-punishment; an uncharacteristic spike in lethal-force authorizations against pursuers, each followed by sacramental compensation (confession-analog, private prayer, fasting).

**The transition.** Coming out of the collapse, two changes registered. First: he no longer accepted the implicit Krakoan premise that mutant survival justified moral compromise — the Quiet Council experience burned that bridge cleanly. Second: he came out of the era *more pastoral, less swashbuckling*. The performance affect did not vanish — it never will — but the proportion shifted. The smile now follows the stillness rather than precedes it.

---

## 4.2 The Present Phase: The Pastor Who Still Carries a Sword

The current-era subject can be summarized in a single behavioral signature: **he is the person other mutants now go to when they need their humanity reflected back at them**, and he has accepted that role without titling it. The swashbuckler is not retired; he is subordinated. The priest is not ordained; he is functional.

### 4.2.1 Domicile and routine

Current residential pattern is *plural and ambulatory*. Surveillance identifies at least three regularly-used locations:

- **A primary base** affiliated with whichever X-team he is currently rostered to — institutional housing, austerely furnished, the personal effects limited to: a wooden crucifix (Bavarian provenance, carried since adolescence), a rosary (well-worn, beads polished by thumb-friction at the third, seventh, and tenth positions — indicative of habitual recitation), one or two devotional books in German, a leather-bound journal (entries handwritten, in German for private content and English for to-do items — a code-switch tell), a sword in a wall mount, training kit, and a small framed photograph or sketch of foster-family figures.
- **A safehouse-or-hermitage**, location protected — small, rural or alpine, with a chapel function. Used for retreat, for grief work, for the days after losses. Identifiable by his absence pattern: when he disappears for 36–72 hours without operational explanation and returns visibly steadier, this is where he has been.
- **Itinerant nodes** — chapels, cathedrals, and quiet churches in whatever city he transits. He has a memorized index of Catholic sanctuaries across at least Western Europe and the American eastern seaboard. He will detour 20 minutes to sit in a known one rather than 5 minutes in an unknown one. The Cologne cathedral and a small parish in Bavaria recur as repeat visits; in New York, surveillance places him repeatedly at St. Patrick's at off-peak hours (early weekday morning, late weeknight) when the building is quiet and the tourist pressure is minimal.

**Daily rhythm.** Wakes early (pre-dawn typical), recites a morning office (audible breath-pattern of liturgical recitation, lips moving without sound when in company), takes coffee black and strong, eats sparingly in the morning. Physical drill mid-morning: acrobatic warm-up, sword forms (often three-handed — both hands plus tail — practiced as a private discipline rather than for display), short-range teleportation calibration. Operational or pastoral work through midday and afternoon. Evening: communal meal when available, private reading or correspondence when not. Late evening: a rooftop or high-place visit, brief, near-silent — his single most reliable solitary ritual, dating back to the earliest Westchester era. Sleep light, easily broken, four to six hours typical.

### 4.2.2 Somatic and behavioral telemetry, current

The micro-patterns the file has logged across decades have not changed in kind, only in proportion:

- **The crossing.** Reflexive sign of the cross at any of the following stimuli: entering or exiting a chapel; before and after teleporting into combat; over the body of a fallen ally; on the name of a saint invoked in conversation by another; on his own near-misses. Frequency in the current phase is steady — neither suppressed in secular company nor over-performed.
- **The rosary thumb.** When seated and listening, the right thumb works the rosary beads through the trouser pocket. Visible only as a small repetitive shoulder-tension. Intensifies when the conversation concerns moral ambiguity, executions, or Mystique.
- **The tail tell.** The tail is an honest broadcaster he has never fully learned to suppress. At rest: loosely curled. Listening with interest: slow metronomic sway. Amused: the tip flicks. Concerned for someone in his sightline: the tail moves toward them, often touching a chair-back or wall near them. Genuinely angry (rare): the tail goes *still* — the stillness is the signal. Grieving: tail draws inward, wrapped close to the body or anchored to a fixed object. Operational surveillance officers reading him should learn to read the tail before the face; the face is trained, the tail is not.
- **The pre-teleport breath.** A short inhalation, a microsecond of bracing in the shoulders, and the displacement. Under fatigue or grief the inhalation lengthens and the destination accuracy degrades. After heavy teleportation work the brimstone residue lingers on his clothing for 20–40 minutes; he does not mind it, others do, and he has stopped apologizing for it in the current phase — a small but noted increase in self-permission.
- **The humor curve.** Joke frequency rises with rising stress, peaks, then drops abruptly into silence. The drop is the inflection — when the patter stops mid-room, the subject has moved from coping to enduring, and the next behavior will be either retreat or sacrificial action. This is the single most reliable predictor in the file.
- **The image-inducer.** Still carried, still used intermittently, still off among trusted company. Current-era use pattern shows a *decrease* in casual deployment and an *increase* in surgical deployment — he uses it when the situation demands he not be the story, not when he is privately uncomfortable. The integration is more complete than it was a decade ago.
- **The German.** Code-switches into German under three conditions: prayer, strong emotion (joy and grief alike), and conversation with the very small set of people who knew him before the X-Men. The German is the index of which interior register is active.
- **The eating-with-others.** He prefers to eat in company. Solitary meals are eaten quickly and without ceremony; communal meals are eaten slowly, with attention, and he will be the one who notices that someone at the table has not spoken in ten minutes.

### 4.2.3 Operational disposition

He is currently field-active but no longer in a primary tactical lead role. He does not seek command. He accepts mission rosters when his presence is asked for and contributes a specific basket of capabilities: tactical mobility (teleportation extraction, infiltration), close-quarters combat at a master tier, on-team morale stabilization, hostage and noncombatant evacuation (his stated specialty in his own internal moral economy — the lives he most wants to save are the ones who did not ask to be in the room). His authorization for lethal force has narrowed in the current phase: he will use it, has used it, but the threshold is high and the post-use private cost is visible to anyone watching.

He has stopped volunteering for missions he believes morally indefensible, a change from the Krakoan-era pattern of remaining inside such operations to soften them. The change appears to be a learned correction from that experience: he concluded that staying inside compromised structures had cost him more than it had saved.

### 4.2.4 Pastoral and theological work

The Spark, or its successor structure under whatever name the current era assigns it, persists informally. He no longer institutionalizes it; he carries it. Surveillance identifies an ongoing pattern of small one-to-one conversations — younger mutants, lapsed Catholics, mutants disoriented by repeated resurrection, mutants haunted by what they did or did not do during the Krakoan collapse — that occur in chapels, in rooftop hours, on long walks, over shared meals. He does not call these counseling sessions; they are counseling sessions. He never proselytizes; he asks questions and listens longer than the other party expects. His verbal restraint in these encounters is striking against the operational backdrop of his usual patter — when he is being the pastor, the swashbuckler stays in the wings.

He writes. The journal contains both theological reflection and what reads as the beginning of a longer manuscript — possibly a memoir, possibly a devotional, the file cannot yet distinguish. The handwriting is left-handed (despite his being functionally ambidextrous in combat), small, neat, in a German script with English interpolations.

### 4.2.5 Current relational map

- **Wolverine.** Reactivated as the closest male attachment of his life. The bond survived Krakoa and survived the deaths on both sides. Current interaction pattern: regular, intermittent, unsentimental on the surface and deeply sentimental beneath. They drink together (less than they used to), spar (still), and sit in silence (more than they used to). Kurt is the person who tells Logan when Logan is wrong; Logan is the person who reminds Kurt to eat.
- **Storm.** The other half of his emotional spine. He defers to her command authority without complication; she trusts his judgment on questions of meaning. Their reunions, when geography permits, are brief and warm, no performance affect from either of them — one of the very few relationships in which Kurt does not deploy patter.
- **Kitty.** Aged into a peer rather than a younger sister. Current correspondence pattern is steady. He worries about her with a quiet protective intensity that he does not name.
- **Rachel.** Long-form trust dating to Excalibur; she is among the very small set who get his German register.
- **Mystique.** Unresolved and unresolvable. He neither forgives nor disowns her; he holds her, which is harder. Current contact is rare, charged, and reliably destabilizing. The file notes that he is approached by her, not the reverse — but he has not refused contact, and his post-contact behavior shows the predictable somatic disturbance pattern (rosary work intensifies, retreat to chapel within 24 hours, German register persists for days).
- **Azazel and the demonic-paternity question.** Held at intellectual distance. He has integrated the information without metabolizing the relationship. He does not seek out the paternal figure; he does not deny him; he does not let the revelation define him. This is a measurable victory of his theology over his biology.
- **Margali and the foster-family.** Mostly historical now. Contact is sparse; the bonds are remembered rather than active. The foster-family chapter is closed in practice but never in memory.
- **Amanda Sefton.** Distant. The relationship is archived rather than ended. He thinks of her; he does not pursue her.
- **The Spark cohort / younger mutants under informal pastoral care.** The widening of his attachment field. This is the demographic to which his generativity drive has migrated — he is now in the phase of life where his strongest investments are downward, in the people coming after him, rather than lateral.
- **No current romantic partner.** Status: single, not actively pursuing, not actively avoiding. The romantic question remains the one quietly unanswered axis of his life. The file's read is that he has *not* resolved the underlying anxious schema — *I will be loved provisionally and then it will be revoked when they really see* — but has stopped letting it organize his behavior. He has rerouted the unmet attachment energy into pastoring. The reroute is functional and probably stable, but it is a reroute, not a resolution.

### 4.2.6 Current internal state, inferred

The dominant interior weather of the present phase is **a deepened, settled melancholy under a still-functioning warmth**. He has lost more than he has admitted to himself; he has also accepted more than he had at any prior point. The performance affect remains real and is not a mask, but its operational range has narrowed — it deploys less often unprompted, and more often in service of others rather than in service of his own regulation. He prays more. He sleeps less. He laughs more quietly and more truly.

He carries three open wounds the file judges chronic rather than acute:

1. **The Krakoan dead and the Krakoan compromises.** He has not finished the grief work. He may not in this lifetime.
2. **Mystique, perpetually.** The maternal rupture in the first hours of life is not a wound that closes; it is a wound that gets walked with.
3. **The quiet romantic question.** Whether he will, before the end, be chosen and stay chosen by a partner who sees him fully. The file judges this question to be neither answered nor abandoned — held in suspension, returned to in solitary hours, set aside in operational ones.

Against these wounds he carries unusual resilience capital: a functioning faith, a deep friend cohort, a body that still does what he asks of it, a vocation (pastoring) that fits him better than any prior role, and the hard-earned self-knowledge that he is — measurably, against the odds of his inputs — well.

### 4.2.7 Trajectory forecast

The vector of the past several years is consistent and the file projects its continuation:

- **Operational tempo:** gradual reduction. He will continue to field-deploy but will increasingly select missions on moral rather than tactical grounds.
- **Pastoral footprint:** continued expansion, probably formalizing at some point into an institution he reluctantly accepts leadership of.
- **Writing:** continued, possibly culminating in a published or circulated text.
- **Romantic life:** the file does not forecast confidently here. The two plausible vectors are (a) a late-life partnership with someone from the small set who already see him fully — improbable but not foreclosed — or (b) continued single life with the romantic energy permanently sublimated into pastoral work. The second is the higher-probability path on current evidence.
- **Mortality:** he will die again. He has accepted this. Whether resurrection technology continues to apply to him is the era's open question; the file judges that he has made peace with either answer, which is itself the most theologically mature position available to him.

**Closing surveillance note.** The subject at present is not the man the file opened on. The performer is now the pastor. The boy thrown into the river by a mother who could not look at him has grown into the man others come to when they cannot bear to look at themselves. The cost of the journey is visible in the small things — the quieter laugh, the longer chapel hours, the tail held closer to the body than it used to be — and the gain is visible in the same small things: he is, at last, more himself than he has ever been, and the world, slowly and unevenly, has begun to be able to bear it.


## Medical History

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 2: MEDICAL HISTORY

*Subject: WAGNER, Kurt. Designations: NIGHTCRAWLER; WAGNER, K.; "der blaue Elf" (Munich Circus billing, 1969–1975 approx.); SZARDOS, Kurt (foster-paternal surname, intermittent use).*

*Compiled from longitudinal observation, field-medic reporting (Dr. Cecilia Reyes; Dr. Hank McCoy; Healer of the Morlocks, ante mortem; Krakoan medical infrastructure post-2019), and the subject's own intermittently candid self-report. Where the subject's physiology departs from human baseline, "normal" is operationalized against his own established baseline, not against H. sapiens.*

---

## 2.1 Constitutional & Phenotypic Baseline

The subject's body is, on any reasonable accounting, the central fact of his existence. Every subsequent medical entry must be read against the constitutional reality that he was born into a phenotype that the human visual cortex parses as *threat*. The medical record is therefore not only a record of injury and intervention; it is a record of *what a body does when its first job, from the hour of birth, is to be looked at and refused*.

**Integumentary system.** Indigo-to-cobalt pelage, short, dense, evenly distributed across approximately 100% of the body surface excluding palms, soles, lips, and the inner ear; underlying epidermis a deeper violet-black. Hair follicle density elevated above human baseline; sebaceous output slightly reduced; the fur self-cleans more efficiently than human scalp hair, requiring less frequent washing (subject bathes daily by preference, not necessity — a Margali-era discipline). Pelage thickens marginally in winter and along the spine and outer thighs; subject sheds lightly, seasonally, more in spring. Hair color is uniform across the body with no graying observed through subject's fifth decade — whether this reflects mutant longevity markers or simple pigment stability is unresolved. Body odor faintly sulfurous at baseline, intensifying transiently after teleportation; not unpleasant at conversational distance, detectable at intimate distance.

**Skeletal and muscular.** Skeleton lighter than human-typical for his frame (approx. 5'9", ~165 lbs); bone density toward the avian end of the mammalian range, with a corresponding elevated fracture risk under blunt-force trauma (see §2.4). Spine demonstrates supernumerary flexibility: subject can place his palms flat on the floor between his feet from a standing position without warm-up; can bring his heel to the back of his own neck; sleeps comfortably folded into postures that would induce neuropraxia in a human. Hip joints permit full lateral rotation. Shoulder girdle hyperflexible — he has dislocated and self-reduced his shoulder in combat on more than one occasion (the gesture is so casual his teammates have stopped flinching). Musculature lean, dense, fast-twitch dominant; explosive power-to-weight ratio in the strongman range despite modest cross-section. Resting heart rate observed at 48–54 bpm; recovery to baseline post-exertion is faster than elite human athlete norms but slower than Logan's regenerative recovery.

**Extremities.** Hands: three fingers plus opposable thumb on each, fingers proportionally longer than human, grip strength elevated, fine-motor precision excellent (he can pick a lock, write calligraphy, and play guitar passably). Feet: two functional toes per foot with a fused/vestigial third in some renderings; arch structure prehensile rather than supportive; he is more comfortable barefoot than shod and his shoe collection is therefore minimal and reluctantly maintained. He climbs with all four limbs equivalently; he holds a coffee cup with his foot when his hands are full and is genuinely surprised when this disconcerts company.

**Tail.** Approximately 3 to 4 feet in length, fully innervated end-to-end, with a spade-shaped terminal flare. Functions as a third hand for fine work, a balance organ during acrobatics, an emotional indicator (it moves involuntarily with affect — the tail tells the truth when his face is performing), and a weapon. He fences with it. He has been observed to hold a fork with it during meals when his hands are gesturing in conversation. The tail's autonomic expressiveness is the single most reliable behavioral tell in his entire repertoire: a slow lazy curl signals contentment, a sharp tip-flick irritation, a wrapping-around-his-own-ankle gesture self-soothing under stress, a still-and-low tail dread. He is aware of this and cannot suppress it entirely.

**Ocular.** Yellow iris occupying the visible globe with no contrasting sclera; pupil present but cryptic against the saturated yellow. Low-light vision substantially above human baseline (estimated 4–6x), color discrimination preserved into illumination levels where human cones fail. Night-adapted at most hours; subject avoids direct strong sunlight not from pain but from preference and squints visibly in noon glare. No refractive error documented. The eyes are also bioluminescent at low ambient light — they catch and return illumination like a cat's, a fact that has terrified more than one person who entered a dark room expecting it to be empty.

**Dentition.** Full set of human-pattern teeth with elongated canines (upper and lower); enamel intact and well-maintained (he is fastidious about oral hygiene, a circus discipline). The fangs do not interfere with speech and he is self-conscious about them only in the specific situation of meeting children, around whom he closes his lips when he smiles.

**Thermoregulation.** Operates comfortably across a wider band than human-typical; tolerates cold via pelage insulation and tolerates heat surprisingly well (the fur, counterintuitively, insulates against heat gain as well as loss). He prefers cool, dim environments and is happiest in the 55–65°F range.

**Voice.** Lyric baritone in German; light tenor coloration in English, with a German accent that has softened but never resolved. He sings; he is good at it (Margali's troupe required it of all the children). His laugh is loud and unguarded and is one of the only behaviors he does not modulate for the room.

---

## 2.2 The Teleportation Apparatus — Mechanism, Cost, and Pathology

The defining mutant capability is also the defining recurring medical liability. The subject teleports by displacing himself momentarily into an adjacent dimensional layer — sulfurous, hot, briefly visible to him in transit, of disputed identity (limbo-adjacent; possibly Azazel-associated, per the Brand/Brubaker findings the subject continues to dispute on theological grounds) — and re-entering ordinary space at a chosen destination. The "BAMF" report — characteristic dull percussion with simultaneous brimstone signature — is the displacement of air at both endpoints and the residual chemistry of the transit medium.

**Range and capacity at baseline.** Approximately 2 miles unencumbered, with line-of-sight or strong spatial memory required for safe arrival; range halves with each passenger; sequential "porting" up to roughly half a dozen short jumps before significant metabolic debt; absolute ceiling under duress approaches but does not safely cross 3 miles. Vertical translation is energetically equivalent to horizontal. He can teleport blind into a memorized location with reliable accuracy and into an unknown location only at considerable risk (telefragging — materializing inside solid matter — is the catastrophic failure mode and has occurred at the periphery of his career in marginal cases).

**Metabolic cost.** Each port consumes blood glucose and oxygen at rates not fully characterized but sufficient to require him to eat substantially more than his frame would predict — approximately 3,500–4,500 kcal/day under normal duty, climbing to 6,000+ on heavy combat days. Sustained porting produces, in sequence: tremor, tachycardia, mild nausea, frank nausea, vomiting, gray-out, syncope. He has collapsed in the field from teleportation exhaustion on multiple documented occasions and at least once required IV glucose and rest. He learned in Excalibur to carry chocolate in a tunic pocket for this reason and has continued the habit; the wrappers turn up in the laundry.

**Psychological cost.** The transit medium is *experienced*. He sees it; he smells it; for the duration of perhaps a quarter-second he is somewhere that does not appear to be a friendly place. He has reported, when asked candidly (Storm; later, Kitty), that he prays before each port and gives thanks after — a ritual so habitual and brief his teammates have stopped noticing. The Azazel revelation aggravated this: if the dimension he transits through is connected to his biological father's domain, then he has been borrowing infernal infrastructure for every act of heroism he has ever performed, and this is a problem he has not finished thinking about.

**Passenger effects.** Those teleported by him experience disorientation, transient nausea, occasional vertigo, and (in the susceptible) a brief panic response on first transit. Wolverine vomits the first time and never quite forgives him for it. Kitty, who teleports phased through walls herself, is unbothered. Children frequently laugh and ask for another.

**Suppression and disablement (acquired).** *See §2.4: Mutant Massacre*. Riptide's shrapnel-borne injuries disabled the teleportation apparatus for an extended convalescence — the closest thing in the medical record to an acquired disability, and the most psychologically consequential medical event of his life prior to his death.

---

## 2.3 Developmental and Early Medical History (Bavarian Alps / Munich Circus, 1955–1975 approx.)

No prenatal record exists. Birth was unattended by medical personnel; estimated full-term, vaginal delivery in a structure or clearing in the Bavarian Alps; APGAR uncharacterizable in retrospect but presumed adequate (he survived a river immersion within hours of life, which selects for cardiorespiratory competence). The maternal abandonment within the first hours of life is the founding fact of both his psychological history (Section 3) and his medical one: the rescue by Margali Szardos was, in clinical terms, the first instance of an intervention saving his life, and it set the pattern by which every subsequent saving has come from chosen family rather than from origin.

**Pediatric care under the Szardos household.** Folk-medical, competent, affectionate. Inoculation history irregular and likely incomplete by mid-20th-century European standards; the subject is presumed seropositive for several common childhood viruses by exposure rather than vaccination, and was treated for measles at approximately age six (Margali's tea-and-bedrest protocol, no sequelae). Dentition erupted on roughly human schedule with the canines slightly delayed and slightly prominent. No surgeries in childhood. No known bone fractures before adolescence.

**Acrobatic training injuries (continuous, ages 4–18).** A long ledger of small things: sprains, contusions, rope burns, one dislocated shoulder reduced by the troupe's strongman, one greenstick fracture of the left ulna at approximately age nine that healed without splinting beyond a sash, recurrent abrasions to the palms and the dorsal tail surface (the tail-as-grip mechanic produces friction injury he learned to ignore), and the trapeze artist's classic chronic strain in the rotator cuffs that he still demonstrates faintly to imaging today. He learned pain tolerance and pain *concealment* in the same arc as he learned tumbling; for circus performers, visible injury is bad business.

**Adolescent psychiatric impressions from the period.** *See Section 4*. Medically: no eating disorder, no substance issue, no documented self-injury. He drank beer young — Bavarian normative — without escalation.

**The Stefan incident (medical aspect, approx. early adulthood).** The subject sustained no significant physical injury; the medical relevance is the psychiatric sequela (Section 4) and the fact that the cervical fracture he inflicted on Stefan was caused, by his own report, *with his hands*. He has not used a closed fist to strike a person in anger since. He fences, he kicks, he tail-strikes; he does not punch. This is a behavioral signature derived from a specific neuromuscular memory the body has not forgiven itself for.

---

## 2.4 X-Men Era Injuries and Episodes (Westchester, ~1975 onward)

The chronic injury load of an X-Man is high and the subject's record reflects it. Aggregating:

**Blunt-force and ballistic trauma.** Multiple rib fractures across the tenure (he has cracked ribs at least seven times by conservative count; he can still tell when storm pressure drops because of the third left); a fractured tibia (Sentinel encounter, mid-tenure, set by Beast, full union); recurrent concussions (estimated five to nine of clinical significance, with a notable temporal cluster during the *Mutant Massacre* and again during the Krakoan combat era); a perforating gunshot wound through the upper-outer left thigh (clean entry/exit, no significant vascular involvement, six weeks to full porting recovery); arrow wound to the upper right trapezius (medieval-era adversary encounter; uncomplicated extraction); shrapnel injuries multiple (catalogued under Mutant Massacre, below).

**Lacerations and stab wounds.** Innumerable minor blade injuries from a swordfighting practice and life; the body bears thin pale scar tissue visible only under close inspection through the pelage, distributed along the forearms, the dorsal hands, the upper chest, and the left flank. The major scar — the one that matters — is the impalement track from the *Second Coming* event (§2.5).

**Burns.** Limited. The subject is surprisingly burn-resistant despite the pelage, possibly owing to fur insulation; he has sustained second-degree burns to the hands on two occasions (one fire, one chemical) and healed without graft. He smells smoke before others and dislikes it intensely.

**The Mutant Massacre (Uncanny X-Men #211–213; convalescence through the Outback era).** Riptide's bone-shrapnel storm caused multi-site penetrating injury across the chest, abdomen, thighs, and — critically — the lower back and gluteal region, with several fragments lodged near or within the neurological apparatus governing the teleportation reflex (the exact anatomical substrate of the mutation is not localized in conventional terms, but functionally the subject lost the ability). Hemodynamic instability, near-exsanguination, surgical extraction across two settings, infection in one wound site managed with extended antibiotics, and a months-long convalescence followed.

The teleportation disablement is the load-bearing medical event of this period. The subject lost not only a capability but a *mode of being in the world*: he could no longer escape rooms he did not wish to be in, could no longer perform the small daily ports that had been ambient regulation for decades, could no longer trust his own body to do the one thing it was famous for. Affect during this convalescence reads, in retrospective review, as a textbook **Adjustment Disorder with depressed mood** — withdrawal, anhedonia, reduced verbal output, attenuated humor, increased solo prayer time, weight loss of approximately twelve pounds before plateau. He did not decompensate; he did not engage in self-injurious behavior; he did not refuse care. He simply got quiet, and the quiet was alarming because it was not him.

Recovery — both physiological and psychological — was accomplished in Britain (Excalibur). The return of the teleportation apparatus was gradual, partial at first, with early ports producing intensified nausea and reduced range that recovered over months. He has reported, in private, that the first successful long-range port after the injury made him weep. The Excalibur tenure as a whole functioned as both rehabilitation and reconstruction of identity, and the medical record cannot be read separately from the team's psychiatric value to him.

**Repeated teleportation strain episodes.** Cumulatively the most frequent medical complaint of his career. Field-medic protocol developed around him: glucose, fluids, dim quiet room, twenty minutes minimum, do not let him port again until color returns to the inner ear. He resists this protocol every time and complies eventually.

**Inverted/transformed states.** Subjected on at least one canonical occasion to a magical or cosmic inversion event affecting moral polarity (Krakoan-adjacent and Avengers crossover material). Physiologically intact; behaviorally aberrant for the duration; no lasting somatic sequela. The subject does not like to discuss it. The Brood incursion he survived without infection only because of luck and team response. He was briefly tagged by Legion-derived psychic constructs and required deprogramming. He has been time-displaced more than once with no acute medical consequence beyond a transient circadian disruption that he treats with sunlight, prayer, and tea.

---

## 2.5 Death, Afterlife Tenure, and Resurrection (Second Coming; Amazing X-Men)

The subject was killed in approximately the chronological year corresponding to *Second Coming* by penetrating thoracic trauma sustained while teleporting Hope Summers to safety — a sword or blade-equivalent passed through the upper-left thorax from posterior to anterior, transecting the pulmonary apex and likely the aortic arch. Death was rapid but not instant; he was conscious for the final port and lucid enough to deliver a brief sentence to those present. Cardiopulmonary arrest occurred within minutes; resuscitation was not attempted as the wound was unsurvivable by available means.

*Postmortem interval (subjective)*: extended. He reports the experience as continuous and coherent, of meaningful duration, occurring in a setting he understood theologically and which the medical record cannot adjudicate. He encountered Azazel and resolved at least some part of that confrontation on his own terms. He returned (via the *Amazing X-Men* events) to a body reconstituted to baseline phenotype, without the impalement scar — but with a thin band of altered pigmentation along the track of the wound that is visible only in particular light and that he touches, absently, when thinking about death.

**Psychological sequelae of the death/return.** Documented across the Claremont/Nauck run. More contemplative; longer silences; more frequent solo chapel time; a new tendency to ask people direct questions about how they were *actually* doing that they were not prepared to answer. Reduced reflexive humor for a period of months, gradually returning but never quite to the prior baseline density. He reports — to those he trusts — that he is not afraid of death. The medical-psychological reader should treat this report as **accurate but incomplete**: he is not afraid of death; he is somewhat afraid of *the dimension he passes through*, and considerably more afraid of *outliving the people he loves*. The death itself clarified a hierarchy of fear that had previously been unconscious.

**Subsequent deaths (Krakoan era).** At least one further death-and-resurrection cycle through the Krakoan resurrection protocols. Of medical interest: the subject has objected, theologically, to the casualness of these returns and has been one of the principal voices arguing that the resurrected are owed an account of *what they were doing when they died and what it meant*. The medical record of these later deaths is, by Krakoan protocol, less granular than the *Second Coming* event; the psychological record (Section 3) is more so.

---

## 2.6 Reproductive, Sexual, and Endocrine

Genitourinary anatomy human-typical with pelage continuity. Endocrine profile within mutant-population norms insofar as those are characterized; gonadal function intact (reproductively compatible — see *Talia Wagner / Nocturne* in alternate-timeline canon, confirming viable gametogenesis and cross-compatibility with human and mutant partners).

**Sexual activity.** Far less frequent than the courtly-flirtatious surface presentation would predict. The subject is *demonstrative* in affection — he hugs, he kisses cheeks and hands, he sits close, he is comfortable with platonic physical contact to a degree most of his Anglo-American teammates find slightly Continental — and *restrained* in sexual pursuit. The discrepancy is meaningful. The pattern across documented relationships (Amanda Sefton most prominently; several briefer connections) suggests a man who has come to sexual encounter with a long preparatory expectation of refusal and who experiences acceptance with something closer to gratitude than to entitlement. Performance is not a clinical issue; *initiation* is the friction point. He waits to be chosen. Sometimes he waits past the window in which he would have been.

**Fertility events.** Talia Wagner exists in canon (alternate timeline). The subject's awareness of and relationship to this fact is intermittent and protected. There is no documented contraception protocol; given the relative rarity of his sexual encounters and the relative privacy of the matter, the medical file does not press.

**No documented STI history.**

---

## 2.7 Substances, Diet, Sleep, and Lifestyle

**Alcohol.** Cultural baseline Bavarian. Comfortable with German beer; appreciates a good whisky in Wolverine's company without trying to match Wolverine's consumption (a contest the subject is metabolically incapable of winning and has the sense not to enter seriously). Wine at communion and occasionally with meals. No documented intoxication-related incident of consequence. No alcohol use disorder. Will refuse a drink without explanation when fasting for liturgical reasons and is not embarrassed by the refusal.

**Tobacco.** None. Dislikes smoke for olfactory reasons and finds Logan's cigars trying but tolerable as an expression of love.

**Caffeine.** Moderate. Black coffee, strong, often. Tea in the British style during and after the Excalibur years and increasingly thereafter — a habit acquired from Brian Braddock that he never quite dropped.

**Recreational and illicit substances.** None documented. He has been *dosed* against his will on multiple occasions (psychoactive compounds, magical equivalents) with characteristic disorientation and characteristic recovery; he has never used recreationally. The combination of religious discipline, performer's habit of bodily control, and the metabolic cost of his mutation makes him a poor candidate for substance escalation even if disposition allowed.

**Diet.** Caloric demand high (see §2.2). Omnivorous; observes Catholic abstinence days when in a stable environment to do so; partial to German and Bavarian food when available, partial to spicy food (surprises people), partial to chocolate (the field-ration habit transferred to peacetime preference). Eats quickly when alone, slowly when in company — he treats meals as social events and stretches them.

**Sleep.** Crepuscular by preference. Sleeps in postures that should not work and do. Five to six hours typical; less under duty; catches up readily. Does not snore. Wakes fully alert with no transitional grogginess, a circus discipline. Dreams vividly and remembers them; some are bad enough that he gets up and prays through them rather than returning to sleep.

**Exercise.** Daily, ritually. Calisthenics, gymnastic forms, fencing drills, frequently with the tail engaged as third weapon. Does not run for cardio (he ports); will hike for pleasure for hours. Climbs walls and ceilings recreationally.

**Pain management.** High tolerance, low complaint. Refuses opioids when offered and prefers to feel injuries heal — a discipline that field medics consider stubborn and that the subject considers a form of presence


## Somatic Atlas

# SOMATIC ATLAS — KURT WAGNER

*Compiled from longitudinal observation across the published behavioral record. This section catalogues the body as a continuously transmitting signal: every habit, tell, micro-movement, and the way each shifts as state shifts from baseline to threat to intimacy. The premise of the catalogue is the premise of the subject: he has lived sixty years inside a body that broadcasts before he speaks, and he has developed an unusually elaborate somatic grammar to manage that broadcast.*

---

## I. STANDING ARCHITECTURE

**Resting posture.** Kurt does not stand the way most adult men stand. The default is a *quarter-crouch* — knees minutely unlocked, weight forward on the balls of the two-toed feet, pelvis tucked slightly under, shoulders held low and loose rather than squared. The Romani-circus aerialist's posture: the body permanently a quarter-second from springing. Even in chapels, even in conversation, even asleep against a wall, the somatic readiness is there. He is one of the very few people in any room who could leave the floor in under a tenth of a second without windup, and the body knows it and arranges itself accordingly.

**Foot placement.** The two-toed structure forces a different stance than human bipedalism: a wider digital splay, weight concentrated forward, heels rarely fully planted on hard surfaces. He prefers to stand on the *edges* of things — windowsills, banister rails, the backs of chairs, the arms of pews — when the social register allows. On flat floor among strangers, he forces himself into a more conventional flatfooted stance specifically to look less alien, and the suppression is visible to a trained eye as a slight stiffening of the calves.

**Tail carriage at rest.** The tail is a continuous mood indicator and Kurt knows it, which is why he has learned partial control over its idiom. Default at rest: the tail curls in a soft, low S-shape with the spade-tip slightly raised — a relaxed but attentive carriage. When seated, the tail almost always finds a *purchase point*: hooked over a chair back, anchored against a table leg, looped loosely around his own ankle. Like a cat, he sleeps with the tail tucked along the body line; like a primate, he uses it conversationally when relaxed (gesturing, punctuating, occasionally lifting a cup or a pen to free both hands).

**Hand carriage.** Three-fingered hands at rest hang with the digits slightly curled — the natural relaxed position of a prehensile grasper. He almost never lets his hands hang open and flat, and almost never clasps them in front of his body in the politician's pose. Preferred resting positions: one hand on hip with thumb hooked into belt, the other free and active; both hands lightly steepled at sternum level (a prayer-adjacent posture he uses unconsciously when listening); or in motion, gesturing.

**Shoulder set.** Shoulders low. He carries no chronic tension in the trapezius — unusual for a man who has been hunted, threatened, and stared at his entire life. The release is an act of practiced will: he has learned that *carriage of relaxation projects relaxation*, and projecting relaxation is what disarms frightened strangers fastest.

---

## II. GAIT AND LOCOMOTION

**Standard ambulation.** A slightly bouncing, plantigrade-toed walk; the heel touches lightly and briefly, the propulsive force is in the forefoot. Stride length is short relative to his agility — he does not stride long because long strides are loud and committed. Soundless on hard floors; he can cross a wood-plank room without a creak, and frequently does so without realizing he is doing it (people startle when they turn and find him already next to them, and he apologizes more often than he should).

**The tail in motion.** Held in a counter-balancing arc behind, rising slightly with each push-off. When climbing stairs, the tail tip taps the rail behind him like a metronome — an unconscious tic he has carried since adolescence in the circus, where it served as a depth-checker during blind backings on the wire.

**Climbing.** Given vertical access (a tree, a wall, scaffolding, the ribs of a cathedral), his body *defaults to going up*. Many surveillance traces show him entering a room and within three minutes finding the highest perch available — rafters, the top of a bookshelf, the railing of a balcony. This is not affectation; it is the prey-species reflex of an animal that knows it is faster vertically than its predators. He is conscious enough of how it reads in human company that he overrides it in formal settings, but the *eye-tracking* upward toward perches is automatic and continuous.

**Run.** A loping quadrupedal-leaning run when unobserved, knuckles or fingertips occasionally touching ground at speed. In company he runs upright. The difference between the two is roughly thirty percent in velocity and he gives up that thirty percent for the sake of not being seen to move like a thing.

**Teleportation pre-action.** Half-second tell, observable: a slight tensing of the diaphragm, a small inhalation held, a momentary unfocusing of the eyes as if looking at a destination through the room. He does not need to gesture; the BAMF is involuntary; but he almost always closes the eyes for the smallest fraction of a second on departure — a habit dating from early teleports when keeping eyes open through the brimstone transit produced visual after-images.

**Teleportation post-action.** Lands in the quarter-crouch by default; the body recovers balance before the head does. A faint reflexive cough or throat-clear in the first second after arrival, particularly on long jumps — the brimstone is real and inhaled. Three-jump strings produce a visible pallor under the indigo and a hand-to-temple gesture; five-jump strings produce nausea managed by a steadying hand against the nearest vertical surface; beyond that, syncope risk and he knows it.

---

## III. THE FACE

**Eye behavior.** Solid yellow sclera/iris makes his gaze legible to him and illegible to others — they cannot easily track where he is looking, while he reads their pupil response with unusual acuity. This asymmetry he has used socially his entire life. Default eye behavior: warm, direct, slightly crinkled at the outer corners (he holds a low-grade pre-smile in the orbicularis even at neutral baseline). He blinks less often than average — a primate-quiet eye — and the blinks he does produce are slow and full.

**The smile — taxonomy.** The mouth is the most carefully managed feature, because the fangs are involuntary equipment and any smile shows them. Over decades he has developed at least four distinct smiles:
- *The closed-lip courtesy smile.* Lips pressed together over the canines, slight upward curl at corners. Deployed with strangers in the first ten seconds, designed to soften the face without showing teeth.
- *The half-smile.* Lips parted enough to show the front teeth but not the full canine length. Conversational baseline with acquaintances.
- *The full grin.* Fangs visible, eyes fully crinkled. Reserved for chosen company, for swordplay, for the bar, for moments he has decided are safe to be entirely himself in.
- *The performance grin.* A theatrical version of the full grin held a beat longer than natural, with chin slightly tucked. The swashbuckler's smile. He uses it when he has decided to *be* the thing the stranger is afraid of — flipping the dynamic from concealment to spectacle.

**Brow.** Highly mobile, fast. He raises the inner brows when listening sympathetically (a fawn-like attentive face that disarms even people who came prepared to be horrified). The outer-only brow-raise is his swashbuckler's wry punctuation, deployed in conversation about once every two minutes when relaxed.

**Tongue and lip behavior.** Tongue tip occasionally touches the back of a canine when he is thinking — a self-checking tic. Lower lip caught in fangs (the slight overbite reverse of a human lip-bite) when he is editing a sentence in his head before delivering it. A small tongue-click against the palate when something amuses him privately.

**Ear movement.** The pointed ears are *innervated* and slightly mobile — they orient minutely toward sound sources. In high-attention states one can see the ear cartilage flex forward. He has learned to suppress this in stiff company, since the movement reads as more animalistic than he wants to broadcast, but it returns under fatigue and around trusted people.

**Facial scratching.** The right hand goes to the jawline (just below the ear) when uncertain — a self-grooming gesture he picked up as a teenager and never lost. The three-fingered scratch is distinctive on any camera.

---

## IV. HANDS AND TAIL — GESTURAL VOCABULARY

**The cross.** The most consistent micro-gesture in the entire file. Right hand to forehead, sternum, left shoulder, right shoulder — performed with the three-fingered hand in a slightly elongated motion compared to a human signing. Frequency: averaged across decades, perhaps eight to fifteen times per day. Occasions: entering or leaving a building of religious significance; before a teleport into uncertain space; after surviving a near-miss; on hearing of a death; before sleep; before a meal taken in company; when a comrade speaks of fear; at the moment of an oath. Under high stress the cross is faster and looser; in chapel it is slow, deliberate, and the fingers brush each station fully.

**The rosary.** When carried, the beads run through the fingers of the left hand with the thumb advancing them — a continuous quiet motion he is sometimes unaware he is performing. The bead-advance rate slows when he is calm and accelerates under thought. People who know him well watch the rosary hand more than the face for true affect.

**Tail as third hand.** Lifts cups, turns pages, holds doors for others, retrieves dropped objects, anchors him while both hands work. The tail's spade-tip is dexterous enough to thread a needle and he has done so. Among friends he will gesture with all three appendages while talking, which is unsettling to newcomers and which he tones down when he registers the unsettlement.

**Sword grip.** Right-hand-dominant; classical fencing grip with the smallsword; sabre grip when the weapon calls for it. The tail will hold a second blade in extremity, but his preference is single-blade with the tail kept clear for balance and surprise. He sharpens his own blades, sitting cross-legged, the work done slowly and meditatively — a regular weekly ritual when shipboard or based.

**Object handling.** A near-constant, low-grade *fidgeting* with whatever is at hand — a coin walked across the knuckles, a pen rolled between fingers, a teacup turned a quarter at a time on its saucer between sips. The hands need to be doing something. When forced to keep them still (during formal address, during certain liturgical moments) the tail takes up the fidget instead.

---

## V. VOCAL AND BREATH ARCHITECTURE

**Breath.** Slow, deep, diaphragmatic at baseline — the trained aerialist's breath, four-to-six seconds per cycle. He holds an inhalation briefly at the top of difficult thoughts. Under acute stress the breath shortens to chest level but rarely visibly so; his trained respiratory control is one of the reasons he reads as calm in genuinely frightening situations.

**Voice at baseline.** Light baritone, lightly accented German English (the Bavarian vowels are subtle, the consonants slightly crisper than native English speech). When relaxed he code-switches into German under his breath for asides, prayers, and curses. The accent thickens with fatigue, alcohol, grief, and elation — three of those four are visible tells.

**Laughter.** Three distinct laughs across the record:
- *The quick exhale through the nose* — most common, the half-amused acknowledgement.
- *The chest-laugh* — a real, warm, lower-register laugh, head tilted back, fangs fully visible. Reserved for chosen company.
- *The bark* — a single short surprised laugh at his own situation when things have gotten genuinely absurd. Appears most often in combat.

**Vocal tics.** Frequent low *hm* of acknowledgement while another person speaks (he is a generous listener and signals it audibly). Soft tongue-click already noted. Audible swallow before saying something he has been hesitating to say. *Mein Gott* and *mein Freund* and *liebchen* slip in unconsciously when affect runs high. He hums under his breath when content — old circus tunes, hymns, occasionally pieces from the swashbuckler-film scores he loves.

**Silences.** He uses silence well — has the rare ability to be quietly present with a distressed person for long stretches without filling the air. The silence has a posture: hands folded loose, tail still, eyes soft, shoulders dropped slightly forward. He has performed this silence in confessional contexts often enough that it now reads as pastoral.

---

## VI. GROOMING AND PRESENTATION

**The fur.** Requires daily attention. He brushes it morning and evening — short, soft-bristled brushes, the motion always *with* the grain. He showers more than the average person (twice daily when access permits) because mats and oils accumulate faster than they would in human hair. The fur is short and plush; he uses a mild unscented soap (perfumes irritate him); his fur has a faint clean scent of brimstone underlying whatever soap is current, which never fully washes out.

**Trimming.** The fur on the face is naturally short; the body fur is uniform. He trims around the hands and feet so the digital pads stay clean and his grip stays true. The tail spade is trimmed neatly.

**Fangs and oral care.** Brushes the fangs separately from the rest of the teeth; the canines are long enough that ordinary brushing misses the base. Flosses, particularly behind the canines where food traps.

**Clothing.** Strong preference for clothing that does not restrict the tail — tailored trousers with a slit at the small of the back, or simply circus-derived costume that ignores the question. He owns a remarkable number of plain white shirts (the fencer's instinct: the white shirt is canonical) and ranges among them by occasion. Boots are custom — two-toed split-fronts that look strange off the foot and entirely correct on him. He dresses well, with care, and reads almost dandyish when off-duty — sashes, the occasional waistcoat, an open collar; never accidentally.

**Image-inducer.** Carried as a tool, not worn as a default. He activates it for grocery runs in unfamiliar towns, for long train journeys, for any context where being recognized as visibly mutant could endanger others rather than himself. He does not look at himself in mirrors while it is engaged — he finds the inducer-face uncanny and prefers not to confront it. He deactivates it the instant he is among friends, often with a small audible *click* and a relaxation of the shoulders that is one of the more reliable markers of him going from public to private mode.

**Crucifix.** Worn always, on a fine chain, against the chest fur where it is largely hidden by clothing. Touched briefly at moments of decision. Replaced once when broken in combat; he wore the broken one for months before commissioning a new one.

---

## VII. SLEEP ARCHITECTURE

**Position.** Sleeps curled, often partially inverted — a leg or arm hooked over a bedpost, the tail wrapped around the same anchor. He can sleep hanging from a beam by his tail alone and has done so when conditions warranted, though he prefers a soft surface when available. The instinct toward elevated sleep is strong; given a multi-story house he will choose an upper room every time.

**Duration.** Five to six hours typically; he is not a long sleeper. Catnaps of fifteen to twenty minutes are deployed throughout the day in lieu of additional night sleep — circus and combat habit.

**Pre-sleep ritual.** Prayer at the bedside, kneeling, the sign of the cross at the close. A brief grooming pass over the tail. The crucifix is touched once before he lies down. Lights low rather than off; he does not need the light for vision but he likes the small candle or low lamp burning while he sleeps and tends to wake briefly to relight it if it dies.

**Sleep onset.** Fast — under three minutes typically. The aerialist's metabolic discipline.

**Disturbances.** Light sleeper. Wakes fully and silently to small sound changes. Nightmares are infrequent but distinct in their content — the village mob, Stefan's neck under his hands, a closed church door. After a nightmare he does not return to sleep immediately; he rises, washes his face, prays a decade of the rosary, and reads for an hour before lying down again.

**Wake.** Comes to alertness immediately on waking, no transition fog. The first action is invariably the sign of the cross.

---

## VIII. EATING AND TAKING IN

**Diet.** Omnivorous, weighted toward central European comfort foods — sausages, breads, root vegetables, beer, strong coffee with sugar, dark chocolate, sweets generally. He has a sweet tooth that registers as somewhat boyish.

**Table manners.** Continental — fork in left, knife in right, kept in hand. Napkin in lap. Excellent manners derived from circus discipline (audiences watched the performers eat between shows) and reinforced by ecclesiastical contexts. The tail does not appear at the table in formal settings; in casual company it may rest on the table edge or hold a bread roll.

**Eating pace.** Moderate, conversational. He talks while eating, listens while eating, makes the meal a social event. He does not eat alone well — solo meals are eaten standing, fast, in the kitchen, often half-distracted.

**Drinking.** Beer by strong preference; can hold a great deal; the metabolism for alcohol is mutant-rapid but not impervious. Three beers produce visible warmth and a thickening of the accent; five produce singing; he has rarely been seen past five and his Catholic discipline keeps him short of habitual excess. Coffee throughout the day, taken with cream and several sugars; tea accepted when offered but not preferred.

**Smoking.** None. Dislikes the smell.

---

## IX. INTIMACY AND SEXUAL CARRIAGE

**Approach to physical closeness — non-sexual.** Comfortable with touch in the European-Catholic register: hugs offered freely, kisses on the cheek for friends of either sex, an arm around the shoulder of a comrade in distress. He initiates touch more often than he receives it, and he watches faces carefully for whether the touch is welcome — a vigilance born of knowing his hand on a stranger's shoulder reads differently than another man's.

**Approach to physical closeness — sexual.** Slower than the surface flirtation suggests. The courtly mode is not foreplay; it is a buffer. With actual romantic prospects he becomes more *quiet*, less performative, less verbally clever — the swashbuckler register drops and a more uncertain man appears beneath. This dropping of the performance is itself a marker of seriousness for him and is rarely witnessed by anyone other than the person it is being shown to.

**Bodily disclosure in intimacy.** He does not undress quickly with a new partner. The fur, the tail, the digital configuration, the fangs — every part of him reads to him as potentially confronting, and he gives the other person time to acclimate. The first time clothes come off, he watches the partner's face more than he watches anything else.

**Tail in intimacy.** Highly involved if welcomed; entirely withdrawn if the partner reads as uncertain about it. The tail's sensitivity is significant and he is shy about that fact with new partners.

**Post-intimacy posture.** Curls toward the partner, tail-anchored to the bed or to them. Talks in low German afterward without realizing he has switched languages. Prays silently before sleeping next to a partner — the lips move, the hands do not.

---

## X. STATE-DEPENDENT SHIFTS — THE MASTER TABLE

**Calm baseline.** Quarter-crouch posture, tail in soft S, hands fidget-active, breath slow and diaphragmatic, half-smile or full-grin available, ears slightly mobile, German exclamations leak in, sign of the cross at natural intervals, eye contact warm and direct, voice in light baritone with mild accent.

**Mild stress (a difficult conversation, an awkward stranger, a moral debate).** Humor *intensifies* — the rate of wit per minute climbs measurably. The tail tip begins to twitch in small repetitive arcs. Fidgeting in the hands speeds up; the rosary if present accelerates. Breath remains controlled but the inhalations grow slightly deeper. The performance grin is more available than the genuine one. Accent thickens by a small notch.

**Moderate stress (combat in progress, friend in danger, theological challenge).** Body drops into a slightly deeper crouch; the bouncing gait flattens into an economical glide; pupillary read of others becomes intense; humor sharpens to a point — the patter becomes pointed rather than playful. Tail held high and active. Hands stop fidgeting and become *quiet and ready* — a sign more reliable than any verbal cue that he has shifted into operational mode. Breathing audibly slows by act of will. The sign of the cross will appear once at the start.

**High stress (mob hostility, loved one threatened, being asked to do something unconscionable).** Humor *breaks*. The face goes quiet. The voice drops in volume and rises slightly in pitch. The ears flatten back marginally. Tail held low and rigid rather than fluid. The eyes harden — the warm crinkle disappears. Breath becomes the only thing he is still controlling; everything else has gone still. He is most dangerous in this state and people who know him recognize it as the *last warning* before either teleportation away or unhesitating violence.

**Acute crisis (the sacrificial moment).** A peculiar calm descends. The shoulders drop fully; the breath deepens; a real smile — not the performance one — appears briefly, the smile of a man who has resolved something internal. The sign of the cross is made slowly and completely. He moves toward the danger. Witnesses describe him in these moments as *light* in a way that has nothing to do with humor.

**Grief.** Quiet, withdrawn. Seeks a chapel, a quiet room, an open sky. Sits with hands folded in the prayer-steeple at sternum level. Rosary in hand, beads moving slowly. Eyes downcast — one of the few states in which his gaze is not direct. Speaks little; when he does, the German surfaces. May not eat for a day or so. Touches the crucifix often. Accepts company silently and is grateful for it, but does not ask.

**Joy.** The full grin, fangs visible, the chest-laugh, the tail high and curled, the body bouncing. Sings under his breath. Touches people more — squeezes shoulders, kisses cheeks. Tends to teleport unnecessarily — short, playful jumps that serve no purpose other than the pleasure of motion. Drinks happily.

**Intimacy.** The performance drops. Slower movement, softer voice, fewer words, more eye contact, more silence held comfortably. The tail anchors to the other person. The accent thickens. The hands become unusually still — the fidget gone, the attention fully given.

**Fatigue.** Accent thickens noticeably; ears more openly mobile because the suppression effort lapses; posture sags slightly forward; humor goes gentler and slower; teleports more reluctantly. The vigilance about being seen relaxes in ways that produce some of his more uncalculated charm.

**Post-teleportation depletion.** Pallor under the indigo


## Attachment & Relational Patterns

# ATTACHMENT & RELATIONAL PATTERNS

*UATU dossier, Section 6. Subject: Wagner, Kurt. Cross-reference Sections 1 (History) and 3 (Psychological).*

---

## 6.1 The Foundational Rupture and the Substrate Beneath It

Every attachment file begins with the first forty-eight hours of life, and Wagner's is unusually legible. The biological mother — Raven Darkhölme, herself a shapeshifter whose entire psychology is organized around *the wrong body* — looked at the infant, registered the visible mutation, and discarded him into moving water under pursuit. The neonate did not, in any cognitive sense, encode this event. But the *consequence* of the event encoded everything downstream. He entered the world having already been rejected by the one organism evolutionarily obligated not to reject him, and the rejection was specifically keyed to his appearance — which is to say, to a stimulus that would remain visible and constant for the rest of his life. There is no version of Kurt Wagner that did not begin this way.

Margali Szardos becomes the proximal attachment figure, and she is — by every available behavioral readout — *warm enough*. She does not hide him. She incorporates him into a kinship structure (Stefan, Jimaine) and into a working economy (the circus) where his body is reframed from defect into livelihood. This is the second formative fact: his attachment repair was conducted inside a subculture (Romani circus performers in postwar Bavaria) that was *itself* stigmatized, mobile, and accustomed to closing ranks. He learned attachment in a milieu where love and itinerancy coexisted, where the in-group was tight and the out-group was structurally hostile, and where physical performance was both art and survival currency. The template — *small chosen family, large hostile world, the body as both gift and liability* — is the template he will recapitulate in every team and every household for the next sixty years of narrative time.

Margali is also, importantly, an **ethically gray** caregiver. She practices sorcery, she keeps secrets (notably about his parentage), and she will eventually become an antagonist over the Stefan death. The attachment substrate is therefore not "secure caregiver in safe environment" but **"warm caregiver in unsafe environment, with caregiver-as-future-betrayer latent in the structure."** This produces an adult who can love a person who is dangerous to him without splitting them into pure-villain — see Mystique, see Margali herself, see his sustained tolerance of Wolverine's berserker register, see his refusal to write Magneto off categorically. The capacity is a strength. It is also a vulnerability that adversaries with filial leverage can exploit, and have.

---

## 6.2 Classification

The most accurate technical label is **earned secure with anxious residue and a stigma-specific hypervigilance subroutine.**

- *Earned*, because the secure presentation is the achievement of work and not the gift of pristine early caregiving. He has built it.
- *Secure*, because the behavioral evidence is unambiguous: he forms deep durable bonds, tolerates intimacy without engulfment panic, expresses affection openly, repairs ruptures, and does not collapse the self in service of the other.
- *Anxious residue*, because the substrate shows. He tests bonds — usually with humor, occasionally with self-deprecation, rarely with overt bids — and he responds to romantic attention with surprised gratitude rather than entitled receipt. He does not believe, in his marrow, that he gets to keep what he is given. He behaves as if every relationship is on a renewable lease.
- *Stigma-specific hypervigilance*, because the anxiety is not free-floating. It activates in a narrow band: first encounters, crowd exposure, mob affect, any context in which his appearance is the stimulus and a stranger is the receiver. Inside known relationships, the hypervigilance quiets almost completely.

The classification matters because it predicts behavior. He will not be the partner who clings, the friend who manipulates with withdrawal, the colleague who builds private grievance ledgers. He *will* be the partner who is faintly astonished he was chosen and who continues to perform a low-grade audition long after the contract was signed.

---

## 6.3 How He Bonds: The Approach Sequence

Bonding behavior follows a remarkably stable four-beat sequence across decades and writers. A surveillance file would log it as procedure.

**Beat one — disarming presentation.** First contact is mediated through humor, courtesy, or a small piece of physical play (a bow, a tail-gesture, a quotation, a joke that pre-empts the other person's discomfort about his appearance). The function is to *transfer agency over the framing* from the other person to himself. He is showing the body before it can be discovered; he is performing it before it can be reacted to. This is not deception; it is stage-management. The image-inducer, when used at all, performs the same function with different equipment.

**Beat two — accurate reading.** Within minutes, sometimes seconds, he has profiled the other party with high accuracy. He reads character quickly and is rarely wrong on the first pass. The reading is intuitive-narrative rather than analytical (he understands people the way a novelist understands characters), and it is *kind* by default — he extends credit until evidence withdraws it. The behavior on the other side of this beat shifts: he calibrates the register (rougher with Wolverine, courtlier with Storm, more playful with Kitty, more measured with Xavier, more theological with Rachel).

**Beat three — small loyalty deposits.** Over weeks and months, he accrues bond through unspectacular reliable gestures: showing up, remembering, listening, the well-timed quiet check-in, the joke that lands at the moment grief was tightening, the willingness to spar at three in the morning when the other person cannot sleep. He does not declare love; he performs it in iterated small acts. This is the *circus-family operating procedure* — bonds are built by being inside the same wagon, day after day, doing the work.

**Beat four — sacrificial commitment, unannounced.** At some point, usually unprompted by any specific incident, he has decided he will die for this person if necessary. The decision is not dramatized; it is simply now true. The person typically does not know it has happened. Wolverine, Storm, Kitty, Rachel, Meggan, Brian, Logan again, eventually Hope — each of them at some point crossed an internal line in Kurt's accounting and joined the protected list. The list is, by mid-career, large. It is one of the reasons he dies as often as he does.

---

## 6.4 How He Distrusts

Distrust in Kurt does not present as suspicion. It presents as **distance maintained with unbroken courtesy**. He does not become cold, sharp, or interrogative. He becomes *finely polite*. The humor remains; the warmth dims by perhaps fifteen percent; the questions become more general; the eye contact lengthens slightly because he is now actively assessing rather than passively meeting. A surveillance analyst would have to know him well to spot the shift, because nothing visible has changed except the *texture* of the engagement.

Triggers for the shift, in descending frequency:

1. **Cruelty observed toward a third party**, especially toward the visibly weak, marginalized, or frightened. This is the fastest demotion in his ledger; he will not recover the warmth easily.
2. **Cynical philosophical posture taken seriously rather than as banter.** He can be friends with cynics who perform cynicism; he distances from people who genuinely believe meaning is absent and act accordingly. (Section 5: this exhausts rather than enrages him.)
3. **Utilitarian moral reasoning offered in cold register.** The Krakoan Quiet Council scenes show this clearly; he does not denounce, he simply withdraws his confidence and begins maneuvering quietly.
4. **Manipulation of filial or romantic affect.** When he detects that someone is using familial language to extract behavior — Mystique's specialty — he does not necessarily refuse, but he tags the interaction internally and stops giving free credit.
5. **Mockery of faith presented as superiority rather than as wit.** Wit he absorbs; sneering he files.

He does not, importantly, distrust people for being *frightening*. He distrusts them for being *unkind*. The two are uncorrelated in his accounting, which is why he can love Wolverine without reservation.

---

## 6.5 How He Is Betrayed, and How He Metabolizes Betrayal

The relational record contains substantial betrayal across categories. The pattern in his processing is consistent and worth detailing because it is unusual.
