- **Withdrawal from group meals.** He will be present at the briefing, present in the field, absent at supper. The meal is where he ordinarily does his most active work as social glue; absenting himself is a powerful negative signal.
- **A specific change in physical carriage.** Ordinarily he occupies vertical and ceiling space — perches, hangs, sits on the backs of chairs and the tops of doorframes. Under stage-two strain he comes down to the floor and stays there. The arboreal presentation is partly play and partly comfort; its disappearance reads as a *retraction of self.*
- **Increased solo physical practice.** Fencing drills alone, often very late, often longer than the body can sustain. The sword work becomes meditative rather than playful — fewer flourishes, more repetition of a single line of cut.
- **Teleportation precision drops in fine detail.** He still arrives where he meant to arrive; he no longer arrives quite where he meant *to stand*. A half-meter off, a degree of rotation wrong. He covers it with a flourish. Storm and Kitty are the two who consistently notice.
- **He starts being kind to Wolverine in a particular way.** Specifically, he starts going to Logan rather than letting Logan come to him, which is the inversion of their ordinary pattern and which Logan, in canon, has registered without naming.

At this stage he will still deny distress if asked directly. He will, however, accept a hand on his shoulder for longer than usual. Touch is the channel through which he can be reached when language has become defensive.

---

## 11.4 Stage Three — The Quiet ("The Light Goes Out of the Room")

The third stage is the one his close circle dreads, because it is the one in which Kurt Wagner *stops being the source of warmth in the room*. The transition is often sudden and is the most diagnostically unambiguous moment in his decompensation arc.

Presentation:

- **Humor falls silent.** Not absent — he will respond if engaged — but no longer initiated. The room loses the man who reliably warms it. To people who have only ever known him operationally this can be the first time they realize how much of the social temperature was him.
- **He becomes punctilious.** Manners sharpen into formality; the courtly register goes from warm to ceremonious. He says *please* and *thank you* with a precision that creates distance. He addresses friends by full name where he ordinarily uses diminutives. This is not coldness; it is the last grip of his discipline holding the structure in place while the affect underneath has begun to detach.
- **Solo prayer becomes very long and very quiet.** Hours in chapel. The rosary worked through fully, more than once, without speaking the words aloud — the lips move, the sound is gone.
- **Sleep degrades.** Either insomnia (sword drills at 3 a.m., a habit observable across multiple eras) or hypersomnia (he sleeps through breakfast, which he never does). Either direction is data.
- **Appetite suppresses.** He eats less, and the things he eats become more austere — the German comfort foods he ordinarily enjoys are replaced by bread, water, coffee, the occasional egg. There is a faintly penitential cast to it that he would deny if named.
- **The image-inducer comes on full-time, even in private quarters.** This is the inverted tell. Ordinarily it is off in safe spaces; in stage three he may wear a human face into his own bedroom. He is, in effect, becoming briefly unable to bear the sight of himself — not because the integrated self-concept has collapsed (it has not) but because being looked at by himself has become exhausting in a specific way. It is a brief, contained, situational failure of acceptance, and it is precisely the kind of micro-collapse a less integrated person would call *normal* and that in him is a flashing red light.
- **Theological argument disappears.** This is the most underrated tell. A regulated Kurt *argues theology* — with Logan, with Kitty, with anyone willing. A stage-three Kurt becomes theologically silent. The internal conversation has gone somewhere the speech cannot reach. When asked a direct question of faith, he gives the catechism answer rather than his own.
- **The tail goes still.** Not held — *still*, in a way that is not its natural state. The most expressive limb on the body becomes a hanging weight. This is the single physical sign most reliable for distinguishing genuine collapse from ordinary fatigue.

The behavioral risk profile in stage three is not violence to others (he does not externalize) and not classical self-harm (he has no incising or substance pattern). The risk is **the unconscious construction of an opportunity to die well**. He becomes, in this state, *more available* for missions of high lethality. He will volunteer for the extraction with the worst odds. He will frame it as tactically obvious — *I teleport, I am the natural choice* — and the framing will be correct. The lethality of the assignment will simply be a feature he does not weigh against the other features. This is the operationally critical observation: **stage-three Kurt is not suicidal in any clinical sense, but he is permeable to opportunities that resolve him out of the situation through service.** The Hope Summers extraction occurred during a stage-three presentation. So, by the longitudinal evidence, did several earlier near-misses that did not result in death only because the situation did not present an opening.

---

## 11.5 Stage Four — The Conversion to Sacrifice

The fourth and terminal stage is not a collapse in the conventional sense. It is a *resolution* — the man comes back online, fully composed, often *radiant*, and proceeds to act. This is the most dangerous presentation in his entire repertoire because **it looks identical to recovery**.

The differentiating markers:

- **A specific clarity in the eyes.** Solid yellow ordinarily reads as alien and warm at once; in the conversion state it reads as alien and very calm. His close circle has learned, over decades, to mistrust this exact calm.
- **He makes amends.** Not in a dramatic register — small ones. Returns a borrowed book. Has a particular conversation he has been putting off. Writes a letter. Visits a person. The pattern is *closing accounts*, performed at a pace and across a breadth that a careful observer can recognize as systematic.
- **Humor returns in a softened, valedictory register.** Less swashbuckling, more affectionate. He becomes notably gentle, especially with the youngest members of whatever team he is on. He blesses children.
- **Theological speech returns, but in the form of *teaching* rather than *arguing*.** He says things he means as final.
- **Tactical generosity.** He volunteers for the assignment whose math does not close.

And then he goes, and does it, and either lives through it because the situation broke in his favor or dies through it because it did not. He has been on both sides of that outcome.

The conversion stage can resolve without death if the action is interrupted — if Storm or Logan or Kitty recognizes the presentation and *grounds* him before the opportunity presents. Grounding takes a specific form: not argument, not concern, but the imposition of a small, ongoing, non-negotiable claim on his presence. Storm asking him to teach a class she could teach herself. Kitty asking him to sit with her while she works. Logan picking a bar fight. The intervention works because it converts him from *the one who is going* into *the one who is needed here*, and he cannot decline the second framing without violating the first principle of his self-concept.

---

## 11.6 Conditions That Produce the Cascade

The cascade does not initiate randomly. The longitudinal record identifies a specific set of triggering conditions, often in combination:

1. **Sustained exposure to mob hostility against mutants.** Not a single incident — single incidents he absorbs and metabolizes. *Sustained* exposure, weeks or months of background fear-rhetoric, accumulates as stage-one strain and is the single most reliable initiator. He does not consciously register the accumulation; the body and the tail do.

2. **Required complicity in utilitarian evil.** Asked, structurally, to participate in or tolerate killings/executions/manipulations he finds morally unjustifiable, *while remaining loyal to the institution doing them.* The Krakoan period is the canonical instance: he could neither leave nor approve, and the unresolved dissonance pushed him through stages one and two over an extended arc before he resolved it constructively by founding Spark. The constructive resolution should not be allowed to obscure how close to stage three he came.

3. **Loss or damage to teleportation.** Identity-integral. Even temporary loss reads as a category of grief. Sustained loss has, historically, produced a full adjustment-disorder presentation (post-Massacre).

4. **The death of someone whose protection he had taken on as a personal charge.** Survivor's guilt around saveable casualties is his most reliably accumulating substrate. Each instance is metabolized; the metabolism is not perfect; the residue compounds.

5. **Direct Mystique exposure of a particular kind** — not antagonism (he handles that) but the moments in which she offers him a fragment of maternal warmth and then withdraws it. This is the one relational input that bypasses his defenses. He cannot tactically clean it; he cannot integrate it; he absorbs it and bleeds.

6. **Romantic loss, particularly when the loss confirms the underlying anxious schema** (she saw him fully and chose to leave). This does not produce dramatic decompensation, but it deepens the dysphoric baseline measurably and durably and reduces his resilience to other inputs.

7. **Forced confrontation with the Stefan question.** Anyone — adversary, therapist, demon, well-meaning friend — who pushes him to re-examine whether he killed Stefan in defense or in rage is wielding the single most destabilizing inquiry available. He has integrated the event; he has not closed the question, and the question reopened produces a fast jump from stage one to stage two.

8. **Theological assault of the right kind.** Mockery slides off. Crude blasphemy slides off. Sustained, intellectually serious nihilism delivered by someone he respects — the argument that the universe is meaningless and his framework is consolation — *exhausts* him in a way that compounds with any of the above.

The cascade is rarely produced by one input. The danger is typically two or three of these inputs co-occurring across a span of months while his social scaffolding is for some reason thinner than usual (a team dispersed, a closest friend absent, a relocation, an institutional reorganization).

---

## 11.7 What Will *Not* Break Him

A counter-mapping, for completeness, because the absence of these failure modes is itself diagnostically significant and should be relied on by anyone planning around him:

- **Direct insult or mockery of his appearance.** Absorbed cleanly. He has done the internal work; the insult lands on the integrated self and finds no purchase.
- **Physical pain, including severe.** Tolerated well; even joked through. Pain is not, for him, an information channel that destabilizes.
- **Fear in combat.** Regulated. He functions at full capacity under acute threat.
- **Tactical defeat.** Metabolized as data, not as identity injury.
- **Being outvoted or overruled.** He does not require institutional vindication; his moral compass is internally referenced.
- **Solitude.** He restores in solitude; he does not deplete in it.
- **Crisis of faith in the sense of doubt.** Doubt is part of his faith's operating system, not a threat to it. He argues himself through doubt routinely and the argument *strengthens* the structure.

The pattern is consistent: **what does not break him is anything that engages his strengths.** What breaks him is the slow attrition of his ability to maintain *meaning* and *grace* in a context that punishes both, especially when he cannot leave the context and cannot fix it.

---

## 11.8 The Recovery Profile

For symmetry, and because recovery patterns are themselves diagnostic: when the cascade is interrupted before stage four, recovery is reliable and follows a predictable shape. It is not fast. It runs months, not weeks.

The sequence reverses approximately in order. The tail moves first — small flicks return before the humor does. Theological argument comes back next, often through Logan baiting him deliberately. Group meals return. The image-inducer goes off in safe spaces again. Vertical occupancy of rooms resumes (he climbs back to the ceiling). Humor returns warm rather than sharp. Prayer shortens and resumes its conversational register. Sleep normalizes. Appetite recovers; the German foods reappear. The last thing to return, and the marker of full recovery, is **unprompted physical play** — the casual fencing-with-the-tail, the somersault over a couch, the act of teleporting across a room for no reason except the joy of arriving. When the play returns, he is back.

The recovery does not require professional intervention. It requires the reconstitution of the chosen-family field around him and a context in which he can again *be useful without being consumed*. Excalibur, in its original configuration, was the canonical recovery environment: small, eccentric, chosen, with room for his courtly register and his theology and his swordplay and his weirdness, and with stakes large enough to matter and small enough not to demand his life weekly.

---

## 11.9 Operational Summary for the File

Kurt Wagner's failure mode is not loud, not externalized, not violent, and not classically self-destructive. It is a four-stage inward collapse that ends, if uninterrupted, in a serene and articulate decision to convert his life into the protection of someone else's, executed with full tactical competence and presented to observers as either heroism or recovery depending on the outcome. The collapse is identifiable in its early stages by anyone trained on his baseline; it is identifiable in its terminal stage only by people who know him well enough to mistrust his calm. The most important single observation in this section, and the one most easily lost in the admiration his behavior generally invites:

**When Kurt Wagner is at his most gracious, most generous, most quietly luminous, and most willing to take the assignment whose math does not close — that is not the apex of his virtue. That is the shape his breaking takes.**

The file should be read with that distinction in hand.


## Trajectory & Forward Assessment

# UATU DOSSIER — KURT WAGNER / "NIGHTCRAWLER"
## Section 9: Trajectory & Forward Assessment

*Forward-looking analytic section. All projections derived from the longitudinal behavioral record assembled in Sections 1–8. Probabilities are qualitative (low / moderate / high / near-certain) and refer to the unfolding decade of subject's life.*

---

### 9.1 The Shape of the Curve to Date

Before projecting forward, the analyst must name the shape of the curve that has already been drawn. Subject's life across the published record describes a **continuous arc from performer to pastor**, with each decade marking a step further from the spotlight and further toward the confessional. The Munich Circus child performed his body for paying audiences. The early X-Man performed his charm for a found family. The Excalibur captain performed competence and warmth for a smaller, weirder cohort. The post-resurrection contemplative began performing *less* and *attending more* — sitting with grief, sitting with theology, sitting with people. The Krakoan founder of Spark stopped performing almost entirely in the institutional sense and instead built a structure in which others could find what he himself had been performing his way toward for forty years: a stable meaning-frame inside which a stigmatized body could be at peace.

The trajectory is therefore not random; it has a vector. **Subject is moving from charm to care, from solo grace to institutional grace, from being-the-light-in-the-room to building-rooms-with-light-in-them.** Every forward projection in this section is a projection along, against, or perpendicular to that vector.

---

### 9.2 The Five Most Likely Forward Developments (Base-Rate Scenarios)

#### 9.2.1 The Pastor Consolidates (probability: high)

The single highest-probability scenario is the continuation of subject's existing vector: deeper investment in his pastoral identity, further development of Spark or a successor theological framework, and a gradual phasing of swashbuckling combat work in favor of moral-conscience work within whatever mutant institutional structure succeeds Krakoa. Expect:

- More frequent positioning as the **interlocutor with the morally compromised** — the person Mystique, Sinister, Exodus, or Magneto-types are sent to *talk to* when no one else can hold the conversation.
- Increasing reluctance to participate in lethal operations; not pacifism, but a rising threshold.
- Authorship — sermons, written theology, a Krakoan-era equivalent of pastoral letters. Subject has the verbal capacity and the inclination; he has not yet produced sustained written work, and the medium is a natural next step.
- A possible formal ordination or recognized clerical status, either reconciled with the Catholic Church (low probability — the institutional barriers are real) or within a mutant-religious framework (moderate-to-high probability).

This scenario is *growth-adjacent but not growth-completing*. It deepens his existing strengths without addressing the residual wounds catalogued in Sections 3 and 5.

#### 9.2.2 A Late, Real Romantic Partnership (probability: moderate)

Subject has reached the point in the developmental arc — post-resurrection, post-Krakoan trauma, mid-life by mutant time-reckoning — where the **courtly-distance pattern with women becomes a live question to him**, not merely to observers. The pattern of unreachable beloveds (Amanda, the various Excalibur-era flirtations, the post-2014 melancholy reconnections) cannot be sustained indefinitely without one of two outcomes: it becomes a settled celibacy he integrates theologically, or it breaks open into an actual durable partnership.

The moderate-probability projection is the latter. The conditions are present: he is no longer hiding from his own form, he has done the post-death contemplative work, he is surrounded by adults who have also done their own developmental labor, and the courtly performance no longer serves him the way it did at thirty. The likely partner profile, derived from his repeated attractor pattern, is **a woman of comparable spiritual seriousness, prior trauma, and tolerance for theatricality** — someone who can match his register and survive his ambient melancholy. Watch for partnerships forming not through the rescue dynamic (his historical mode) but through *theological or pastoral collaboration* — the working partnership that becomes intimate.

If this consolidates, it is the single most growth-productive development available to him. If it fails to consolidate, the courtly mode hardens into clerical celibacy and the question is foreclosed rather than answered.

#### 9.2.3 A Reckoning with Mystique (probability: high; timing uncertain)

The Mystique relationship is the largest unresolved arc in the file and the one element subject has not yet been able to integrate cleanly. The forward record will almost certainly contain at least one more major confrontation, and possibly a final one. The shape of that confrontation has three plausible variants:

- **The mercy variant.** Subject extends grace at a moment Mystique does not expect and cannot weaponize; she is altered by it (transiently or permanently); the relationship achieves a low-grade armistice. This is the variant most consistent with subject's character and most narratively earned. Probability: moderate-to-high.
- **The repudiation variant.** Mystique commits an act subject cannot integrate (harm to Kitty, to Logan, to the broader mutant project beyond reversal); subject finally and explicitly disowns her. This would be a developmental loss disguised as a developmental gain — the *capacity to hold ambivalence with Mystique is one of his most mature features*, and severing it would represent the splitting defense he has otherwise been free of. Probability: low-to-moderate.
- **The deathbed variant.** One of them dies (again, in mutant terms — but in some structurally final way) and the other is present. Probability: moderate. This is the variant that does the most psychological work, because it forces subject to articulate what he has spent forty years refusing to articulate: *what he actually feels about the woman who threw him into a river*.

#### 9.2.4 Another Sacrificial Death (probability: high over a long enough horizon)

Subject's altruism profile (Section 3) and his demonstrated willingness to convert his existence into protection-for-others (Sections 3, 5) make additional sacrificial deaths near-inevitable on a long horizon. The clinical question is not *whether* but *whether the pattern remains adaptive or becomes overdetermined*. Each successive sacrifice raises the probability that the underlying motive includes the unanswered question — *am I lovable enough to stay for?* — and the analytic concern is that a fourth or fifth such episode begins to look less like principled altruism and more like a settled relationship to his own continuance that should worry his confessor.

**The fork point here is whether subject ever, in a documented private moment, says aloud that he does not want to die again.** That sentence has not yet appeared in the record. Its appearance would be a major developmental marker.

#### 9.2.5 The Azazel Inheritance Re-Surfaces (probability: moderate)

The Azazel retcon was tonally rejected by subject and by most subsequent writers, but it has never been erased and the genetic-theological premise remains a live narrative asset. Forward developments are likely to include at least one further episode in which subject is forced to confront either Azazel himself, a half-sibling (Abyss, others), or a teleportation-dimension question that requires him to engage the demonic patrimony rather than dismiss it. The growth-productive resolution is integration without acceptance — *acknowledging the biology without accepting the meaning Azazel assigns to it*. The catastrophic resolution is being manipulated into a moment of demonic-coded action (a kill performed in the brimstone dimension, an act of teleportation weaponization) that re-cues the Stefan trauma and reopens the question of whether his form and his evil are linked. Adversaries who understand his file will attempt this.

---

### 9.3 The Open Questions

A forward dossier is honest about what it does not know. The following questions are genuinely undetermined by the record and will shape the next decade more than any plot-level event:

1. **Does he ever stop performing lightness in private?** The reaction-formation overlay (Section 3) is so well-integrated that even he may not fully see it. The question is whether age, partnership, or sustained contemplative practice eventually allow him to be visibly tired, visibly sad, visibly afraid *with his friends* rather than only in chapels.
2. **Does the Catholic identity survive a final break with the institutional Church, or does it require one?** Subject's faith is operational rather than aesthetic, but he has never been formally repudiated by Rome and has never formally repudiated Rome. A forced choice is overdue.
3. **Can he be a father in a stable, present way?** The Talia Wagner / Nocturne relationship is alternate-timeline and structurally distant. A primary-timeline parenthood, whether biological or adoptive (a Krakoan-orphan ward is the most plausible vector), is a developmental experience he has not yet had and which would test every romantic-courtly idealization he carries about family.
4. **What does he do when he is no longer needed as a combatant?** Subject's physical excellence has been continuous since adolescence. The decade in which it begins to decline — and for a mutant of his power profile that decade is approaching, even accounting for healing-factor-adjacent resilience — is the decade in which his sense of self will be tested in a way the Mutant Massacre injuries only previewed.
5. **Can he build something that survives him?** Spark was a beginning. The question is whether subject is a founder-figure (whose work outlives him) or a charismatic-figure (whose work depends on his presence). The honest assessment is that the record does not yet tell us.

---

### 9.4 Fork Points: The Specific Decisions That Will Decide the Trajectory

Forward outcomes are not produced by background variables; they are produced by specific decisions taken at specific moments. The file identifies the following fork points as decisive within the next decade of subject's life:

**Fork 1 — The Next Time Mystique Asks Him for Something He Should Refuse.** The historical record shows subject vulnerable to filial-residue manipulation by Mystique. The next instance is the test of whether the contemplative post-death work has reached this corner of his psyche. *Refusal-with-grace* moves him to a more integrated stage; *refusal-with-coldness* indicates splitting has begun; *acceptance* indicates the work is incomplete.

**Fork 2 — The Next Mob Scene.** Subject's single most reliable dysregulator (Section 5) is mass-fear directed at his appearance. The next major instance — anti-mutant rally, public exposure incident, hostile civilian crowd in an operational context — is the test of whether decades of integration have raised the dysregulation threshold or whether the village mob remains the permanent template. *Holding affect and responding pastorally* indicates genuine consolidation; *retreat-by-teleportation* indicates the wound remains live but managed; *uncharacteristic anger* indicates decompensation under accumulated load.

**Fork 3 — The First Time He Is Offered Ordination or Its Equivalent.** Whether Catholic, Krakoan-religious, or something not yet named, the institutional-recognition offer will come. *Accepting* moves him decisively into the pastor identity and forecloses certain romantic and combat-operational futures. *Refusing* preserves his hybridity at the cost of clarity. *Deferring* — his most likely response — is itself a decision that signals which questions remain open for him.

**Fork 4 — The First Time He Says No to a Sacrifice He Could Have Made.** The single most growth-productive moment available to him is the moment he chooses *not* to die for someone he could have died for, on the principled ground that his continued life serves the project better than his death. This would be a major developmental marker and would indicate that the altruism profile has been examined and tempered rather than left as a settled reflex.

**Fork 5 — The First Time He Tells Someone He Is Tired.** Mundane, decisive. The performed lightness has not yet broken open in a sustained way with a peer. The peer most likely to receive that disclosure is Logan; the peer who would most change as a result of receiving it is Storm; the peer whose receiving it would mean the most developmentally is a romantic partner. Watch for it.

**Fork 6 — A Forced Choice Between Faith and Community.** Subject has been fortunate that his theological commitments and his communal loyalties have rarely been in direct opposition. They will eventually be. The Krakoan executions arc was a preview; a fuller test is overdue. *Choosing faith* makes him a prophet at the cost of his place; *choosing community* makes him a leader at the cost of his clarity; *finding a third path* is his characteristic move and the one he is most practiced at, but the third path is not always available.

---

### 9.5 Growth Vector vs. Catastrophe Vector

#### What Pushes Him Toward Growth

- **Sustained contemplative practice with a confessor or spiritual director who is not himself a mutant.** Subject's pastoral work is partly compensatory; he needs to be the one *receiving* care to complete the developmental loop. An external confessor — ideally human, ideally without stake in mutant politics — would be the single most growth-productive relationship he could add to his life.
- **A romantic partnership that survives the disclosure of his ambient melancholy.** Not a partnership in which he performs lightness for a loving audience, but one in which the lightness is allowed to drop.
- **Mentorship of a younger mutant whose stigma profile resembles his own.** A visibly-mutated adolescent who needs the integration work subject has already done. This is the generativity-stage task in his developmental schedule and the record suggests he is ready for it. Watch for the relationship that forms in this slot; it will be load-bearing.
- **A specific, articulated decision to live rather than to die for the team.** Section 9.4, Fork 4. The single most important interior development available to him.
- **Reconciliation work with the Romani-circus chapter of his life.** Subject's foster-family origins are underexamined in his contemplative practice. Returning to that material — Margali's antagonism, Stefan's death, the Munich Circus audiences — without the protective distance of swashbuckler patter would constitute genuine trauma integration.

#### What Pushes Him Toward Catastrophe

- **Repeated sacrificial deaths without an interceding interior reckoning.** Each one further normalizes the pattern; each one further blurs the line between altruism and a quiet relationship to his own dispensability that he has never named.
- **A Mystique act he cannot integrate.** Forcing the repudiation variant of Section 9.2.3 would cost him the mature ambivalence-holding that is one of his rarest features. The split, once made, is hard to unmake.
- **A successful Azazel-coded manipulation.** An adversary who reads the file accurately and stages an incident that re-cues both the Stefan trauma *and* the demonic-patrimony anxiety in the same operational moment. This is the highest-leverage attack available against him and the one he is least defended against.
- **Institutional clerical authority granted prematurely.** If he accepts a pastoral role before fully completing the personal integration work, he will become a *functioning* pastor with a *concealed* private deficit, and the gap between public role and private state will widen rather than close. This is the failure mode of clergy generally and subject has the temperament to fail in exactly this direction.
- **The death of Storm or of Logan in a context where he could not intervene.** Either loss would land hard. The combination, or either in close succession with another major loss, would risk a depressive episode of greater duration than anything in the existing record. His faith would hold; his affect would not.
- **A sustained period without operational purpose.** Subject's compensations require a structure to operate within. An extended interregnum — no team, no congregation, no clear role — would activate the post-Mutant-Massacre pattern (Section 4: Adjustment Disorder with depressed mood) and possibly something deeper given the absence of the Excalibur-style rescue that interrupted the earlier episode.

---

### 9.6 The Slow Catastrophe (the failure mode he is least likely to see coming)

Acute catastrophes are visible and subject will meet them with his existing repertoire. The failure mode the file is most concerned with is **slow**: the gradual hardening of the pastor identity into a role he can no longer step out of, the gradual narrowing of the romantic possibility space into a settled and uninterrogated celibacy, the gradual sublimation of every personal need into communal service, and the gradual replacement of *being* Kurt Wagner with *being the person Kurt Wagner is for everyone else*.

This is not a disorder. It is not a crisis. It is the characteristic failure mode of a particular kind of high-functioning altruist with a religious vocation and a self-worth schema indexed to usefulness. Subject is at moderate-to-high risk for this trajectory precisely because none of its components would be alarming individually and because the people around him would experience the resulting Kurt as *better* than the current one — calmer, more patient, more available, more saintly. The cost would be borne entirely interiorly and would be visible, if at all, only in a slight further dimming of the swashbuckler register and a slight further deepening of the chapel hours.

The countervailing factor is that subject has, across the record, demonstrated an unusual capacity for *seeing his own patterns when they are named*. He is not defensive about psychological self-knowledge. A confessor, a partner, or a sufficiently brave friend who said the sentence — *Kurt, you are disappearing into the work* — would in all probability be heard. The forward question is whether anyone in his life is positioned to say it and willing to say it.

---

### 9.7 Summary Projection

Subject's most likely ten-year trajectory is **continued consolidation along the pastor vector**, with moderate probability of a late durable partnership, high probability of further confrontation with Mystique, near-certainty of at least one additional sacrificial-death episode, and a quiet but real risk of the slow-catastrophe failure mode described above. The acute-catastrophe risk is low; the resilience capital is high; the interior question of whether he will *let himself be the recipient of care rather than only the provider of it* remains the single most decisive variable in the file.

**The headline finding for this section:** subject is not at risk of breaking. He is at risk of refining himself into a shape so useful to others that the question of his own happiness ceases to be asked — by them, and eventually by him. The growth path requires someone to keep asking it. The dossier recommends that, whatever else is done with this file, that question be kept open on his behalf.

— UATU, ends Section 9.
